Specifications that define WebIDL content (WHATWG perspective)

May 10, 2018

Reffy is a spec exploration tool. It crawls a list of specifications to study the WebIDL content, the links that they contain, and the references that these specifications contain.

Accelerated Shape Detection in Images

Spec info

  • Crawled version: Initial URL (4 April 2018)
  • Repository: GitHub wicg/shape-detection-api
  • Shortname: no shortname

Potential issue(s)

  • Missing references for WebIDL names:
    • Point2D defined in MediaStream Image Capture
  • Missing references for links:
    • https://w3c.github.io/mediacapture-image/
  • Inconsistent references for links:
    • https://www.w3.org/TR/2dcontext/, related reference "HTML" uses URL https://html.spec.whatwg.org/multipage/

Known dependencies on this specification

No normative reference to this spec from other specs.

  • Accelerated Shape Detection in Images

  • Editor's Draft: https://w3c.github.io/accelerometer/
  • Latest published version: https://www.w3.org/TR/accelerometer/
  • Latest published status: Candidate Recommendation
  • Repository: GitHub w3c/accelerometer
  • Shortname: accelerometer

Potential issue(s)

  • Missing references for links:
    • https://w3c.github.io/motion-sensors/
    • https://w3c.github.io/sensors/usecases.html
  • Inconsistent references for links:
    • https://www.w3.org/TR/screen-orientation/, related reference "SCREEN-ORIENTATION" uses URL https://w3c.github.io/screen-orientation/

  • Crawled version: Editor's Draft (24 April 2018)
  • Editor's Draft: https://w3c.github.io/ServiceWorker/v1/
  • Latest published version: https://www.w3.org/TR/service-workers-1/
  • Latest published status: Working Draft
  • Repository: GitHub w3c/ServiceWorker
  • Shortname: service-workers-1

Potential issue(s)

  • Unknown WebIDL names used: VisibilityState
  • WebIDL names also defined elsewhere:
    • Worker also defined in HTML Standard
  • Missing references for links:
    • https://w3c.github.io/push-api/
  • Inconsistent references for links:
    • https://w3c.github.io/webappsec-referrer-policy/, related reference "REFERRER-POLICY" uses URL https://www.w3.org/TR/referrer-policy/
    • https://w3c.github.io/webappsec-secure-contexts/, related reference "SECURE-CONTEXTS" uses URL https://www.w3.org/TR/secure-contexts/
    • https://w3c.github.io/webappsec-csp/, related reference "CSP-3" uses URL https://www.w3.org/TR/CSP3/
